      <section>
        <div id="title">
          <h1>Can Dunks Replace the Archaic Point System</h1>
          <p>This analysis will look into how important dunks and dunk defense are to a game’s outcome</p>
          <hr>
          <span class="credits left">Project maintained by <a href="https://github.com/mprego">mprego</a></span>
          <span class="credits right">Hosted on GitHub Pages &mdash; Theme by <a href="https://twitter.com/michigangraham">mattgraham</a></span>
        </div>

        <h3>
<a id="basketball-blog" class="anchor" href="#basketball-blog" aria-hidden="true"><span aria-hidden="true" class="octicon octicon-link"></span></a>Basketball Blog</h3>

<h2>
Analysis of Dunk and Game Outcomes
</h2>

<p>
To represent dunks as a score, i’ve created a metric that rewards dunks and penalizes missed dunks:<br>
<i>Dunk Score = Made Dunks - Missed Dunks (either by fault of offensive player or by defensive block)</i>
<br>
<br>
Using shot analysis on NBA.com, this metric is tallied up for each team in each game in the 2014-2015 NBA season.  
<br>
<br>
Looking at the Dunk Score vs the actual score, there is a slight correlation of 0.13 (Orange is home team and Blue is away team):
</p>
